```text
pub fn signinum_core::collect_indexed_batch_results<T, E, B, F>(usize, alloc::vec::Vec<signinum_core::batch::IndexedBatchResult<T, E>>, F) -> core::result::Result<alloc::vec::Vec<T>, B> where F: core::ops::function::FnOnce(usize, E) -> B
pub fn signinum_core::copy_tight_pixels_to_strided_output(&[u8], (u32, u32), signinum_core::pixel::PixelFormat, &mut [u8], usize) -> core::result::Result<(), signinum_core::error::BufferError>
pub fn signinum_core::strided_output_len((u32, u32), usize, signinum_core::pixel::PixelFormat) -> core::result::Result<usize, signinum_core::error::BufferError>
pub fn signinum_core::tile_batch_worker_count(usize, signinum_core::batch::TileBatchOptions, usize) -> usize
pub fn signinum_core::validate_strided_output_buffer((u32, u32), usize, usize, signinum_core::pixel::PixelFormat) -> core::result::Result<(), signinum_core::error::BufferError>
pub type signinum_core::IndexedBatchResult<T, E> = (usize, core::result::Result<T, E>)
```

## `signinum-cli`

`signinum-cli` is a binary package. Its stable command, stdout/stderr, and exit-code contract is documented in `docs/stable-api-1.0.md`.
